  </table>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">NEWPORT
BEACH, Calif. and SALT LAKE CITY, August 16, 2021 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) &mdash; <B><U>Verb Technology Company, Inc.</U> (Nasdaq: VERB) (&ldquo;VERB&rdquo;
or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;)</B>, the leader in interactive video-based sales enablement applications, including interactive livestream
ecommerce, webinar, CRM and marketing applications for entrepreneurs and enterprises, today reported financial and operating results
for the second quarter and six months ending June 30, 2021.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Management
Commentary</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;It&rsquo;s
been a very exciting time for us at VERB. Since we last reported in May, we have made several milestone announcements that highlight
our solid progress in delivering best-in-class sales-driving technology and applications,&rdquo; said Rory J. Cutaia, CEO of VERB. &ldquo;We
released verbMAIL for the Microsoft Outlook platform, a revolutionary video email solution that makes our proprietary interactive video
technology available to over one billion Outlook users, turning a favorite contact management tool into a favorite sales tool. We announced
a major partnership with Market America Worldwide | SHOP.COM, for the deployment of our verbLIVE livestream ecommerce application to
over 100,000 distributors globally, and launched it with our Attribution feature throughout Asia, Europe and North America in July. We
also announced a similar partnership this quarter with NewAge, Inc., a direct-to-consumer (D2C) sales company, to add up to 600,000 distributors
on our platform in 75 countries.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;And
we introduced PULSE, our newest sales enablement platform feature. It&rsquo;s like a sales coach in your pocket tracking your interactions
with your prospects and telling you what to do next to close that sale.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;For
the second quarter, our SaaS recurring revenue grew 26% year over year and 10% from the previous quarter. Our results do not include
contributions from any of the recently announced products and partnerships, but we expect these to produce a positive revenue impact
in the coming quarters.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;We
                                            believe that our technology and suite of sales enablement solutions give us a clear competitive
                                            advantage and position us to lead the burgeoning high-growth livestream ecommerce sector,
                                            which has already seen tremendous success in Asia and which we believe is set to gain ground
                                            in the U.S. and other markets. In addition to launching verbLIVE with Market America and
                                            multiple sales applications with NewAge, Inc., we are continuing to build a robust sales
                                            pipeline targeting larger businesses that can accelerate product adoption and boost annual
                                            recurring revenues.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;We
continue to improve on our offerings, fine-tuning and elevating, and adding new, value-enhancing, innovative features and products that
will continue to allow us to deliver the industry leading sales enablement tools our clients and customers have come to expect from us.
We are also adding sales and marketing professionals to respond to the growing demand we are cultivating while simultaneously increasing
product penetration among existing clients. We are continuing to deliver paradigm-shifting technology and products which represent long-term,
value-creating revenue catalysts that drive our growth and increase shareholder value. We are excited to report on our continued progress
for the remainder of the year.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Second
Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Recent Company Highlights </B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

    SaaS recurring revenue (a component of Total Digital revenue) was $1.6 million, up 26% year over year, and up 10% over Q1 2021.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

    recurring revenue as a percentage of Total Digital revenue was 88%, compared with 76% for the same period last year and up over the
    81% we reported in Q1 2021.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
    Digital revenue of approx. $1.8 million, up 8% year over year. </FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
    combined revenue of approx. $2.4 million represents the 10% growth in our SaaS recurring revenue over last quarter and 26% over last
    year, and a reduction in revenue from the legacy printing and fulfillment side of our business of approximately $400K since last
    year as that component of our business is driven by our clients&rsquo; in-person conferences and sales events which were essentially
    non-existent due to the continuing effects of COVID. </FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">

    numbers do NOT include the expanded revenue we expect to recognize from existing clients who have recently launched and those that
    are about to launch verbLIVE with Attribution, which should add not less than an additional $1 million, conservatively, in annual

  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">

    user downloads now at 2.8M, up more than 75% over the 1.6M reported in same period last year, and up from approximately 2.0M as of
    May 13, 2021, which represents an increase of 40% in just the last 90 days.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">

    to the development of verbLIVE, VERB&rsquo;s new Attribution feature, product enhancements to verbCRM, the Microsoft Outlook integration
    and the forthcoming new Marketplace platform, among other as yet unannounced features and products.</FONT></TD></TR>

    and administrative expenses were $6.5 million, compared with $4.0 million for the same period last year, with the increase attributed
    to labor-related costs to support growth, marketing expenses, professional services, as well as expenses related to an additional
    quarter of SoloFire operations following the acquisition.</FONT></TD></TR>

    own livestreaming channel to easily demonstrate and sell products to current or potential customers at any time.</FONT></TD></TR>

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Partnered
    with NewAge, Inc. for delivery of their sales enablement app for use by up to 600,000 of their brand partners and distributors in
    75 countries to help increase customer engagement and sales conversion rates. The app includes customer relationship, content, and
    learning management systems, and they are expected to add verbLIVE, our livestream shopping app in September 2021.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Introduced
    a new, powerful Attribution feature to verbLIVE, which adds affiliate marketing technology to allow anyone to receive credit for
    purchases made by their referrals to verbLIVE sessions hosted by others, which we expect will drive attendance and revenues exponentially.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Introduced
    PULSE, an AI/BI-based feature set that tracks prospect interactions then educates salespeople while it automates the selling process</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">New
    VERB platform [codename] Marketplace, a new 24/7 online shopping destination, is in active beta testing with multiple retailers.
    Simultaneous interactive livestream sessions hosted by retailers, consumer brands, and influencers across numerous categories will
    comprise Marketplace, creating a fun, engaging and social shopping experience for consumers and hosts alike.</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Six
Months Ended Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; background-color: white; color: #535D60"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

  <TR STYLE="letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt; width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt; width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD>

    SaaS recurring revenue (a component of Total Digital revenue) was $3.1 million, up 31% year over year</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD>

    recurring revenue as a percentage of Total Digital revenue was 85%, compared with 74% for the first 6 months of 2020.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Total
    Digital revenue of approx. $3.6 million, up 15% year over year. </FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Research
    and development expenses were $6.1 million, compared with $2.9 million for the same period last year, with the increase attributed
    to the development of verbLIVE, VERB&rsquo;s new Attribution feature, product enhancements to verbCRM, the Microsoft Outlook integration,
    the forthcoming new Marketplace platform, among other as yet unannounced features and products.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify; letter-spacing: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">General
    and administrative expenses were $13.9 million, compared with $7.5 million for the same period last year, with the increase attributed
    to non-cash stock compensation expense, labor-related costs to support growth, professional services, marketing expenses, as well
    as expenses related to SoloFire operations following the acquisition.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; letter-spacing: 0pt; vertical-align: top">

    to the end of the quarter, the Company converted all remaining 1,706 preferred shares into shares of the Company&rsquo;s common stock.&nbsp;&nbsp;As
    a result, there are no more shares of preferred stock outstanding. </FONT></TD></TR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Verb
Technology Company, Inc. (Nasdaq: VERB) transforms how businesses attract and engage customers. The Company&rsquo;s Software-as-a-Service,
or SaaS, platform is based on its proprietary interactive video technology, and comprises a suite of sales enablement business software
products offered on a subscription basis. Its software applications are available in over 60 countries and in more than 48 languages
to large enterprise and small business sales teams that need affordable, easy-to-use, and quick-to-get-results sales tools. Available
in both mobile and desktop versions, the applications are offered as a fully integrated suite, as well as on a standalone basis, and
include verbCRM (Customer Relationship Management application), verbLIVE (Interactive Livestream eCommerce and Video Webinar application),
verbTEAMS (a Self On-boarding version of verbCRM with built-in verbLIVE and Salesforce synchronization for small businesses and solo
entrepreneurs), verbLEARN (Learning Management System application), and verbMAIL (an interactive video mail solution integrated seamlessly
into Microsoft Outlook). The Company has offices in California and Utah. For more information, please visit: www.verb.tech.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Most
of the world is now online and soon the entire planet will be online with unlimited affordable high-speed mobile access through 5G technologies
everywhere and all the time.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">What
are they doing online? They&rsquo;re watching videos. They&rsquo;re creating and sending videos, and they&rsquo;re shopping. Look, I
think we&rsquo;re pretty smart, but it doesn&rsquo;t take a genius to see that those things will converge. Of course they will, it&rsquo;s
inevitable. Think about some of these data points. More and more people are cutting the cable TV cord and watching content online. Millennials
are not even buying TVs. They&rsquo;re consuming video content on their mobile devices. Why do you think you&rsquo;re seeing Apple developing
their own content for online consumption? Amazon Prime, Netflix, Disney Plus and HBO Max are now distributing the latest studio films
online. At the same time, they&rsquo;re putting them in theaters. Heck, even Salesforce is now getting into the content creation game.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">But
no, it&rsquo;s not interactive clickable content. We&rsquo;re just way ahead of the big incumbents who&rsquo;ve gotten very comfortable
enjoying the massive growth they&rsquo;ve achieved, and they&rsquo;re afraid to venture into anything new that might impact the status
quo. That&rsquo;s our opportunity.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">When
you do watch something on TV, what&rsquo;s in your hand? Your mobile device. What are you doing? You&rsquo;re shopping. When you record
a show or a movie and the commercials come on? What are you doing? You&rsquo;re hitting the fast forward button. If you&rsquo;re a sponsor
of that content or an advertiser trying to promote and sell your products or services, and you&rsquo;re relying on the Nielsen ratings,
or some other rating service to know if you&rsquo;re getting an ROI on that spend? Well, let me share a secret with you. You&rsquo;re
not.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Why?
Well, it comes down to a growing sentiment that I&rsquo;ve been talking about for a long time. People want to buy, they want to shop,
but they don&rsquo;t want to be sold. Let them click in the video to get more information about your product or service. Let them click
and download that that brochure or give them a click to buy now button in the video and let them purchase that product they see featured
in that video. Play to that impulse buy propensity that Jeff Bezos mastered. He conditioned the whole world to embrace the convenience
of one-click buying, eliminating friction from the sales process.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Our
technology delivers that capability right in the videos. Whether they&rsquo;re videos you record on your phone or share through email,
text or post online or live broadcasts, livestream video events or shows anyone can host using our verbLIVE platform. This is the convergence
of video and shopability that I&rsquo;ve been talking about for years.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">The
market is still in its earliest stage, but now it&rsquo;s accelerating, especially over the past year. People are now seeing it; the
investment community is now getting it; that&rsquo;s why our shareholder base has exploded. By the way, so has our user base. We&rsquo;re
now at almost 3 million downloads of our apps; I think about 2.8 million, and our sponsors and advertisers begin to realize that this
technology is available, Verb Technology that allows them to know in real-time how many people are actually watching in that moment,
who&rsquo;s watching, what did they click on? What did they buy? What did they spend? They can actually measure that ROI, truly measure
it.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">That&rsquo;s
when the money behind those sponsors and advertisers will demand that content creators adopt this technology. That&rsquo;s when anybody
selling anything will adopt this technology. Every user of this technology, of our applications, becomes an extension of our marketing
team, because simply by using our technology, by creating videos, adding the clickable buttons, making them shoppable, and sharing those
videos with scores of others, they unknowingly become Verb volunteer salespeople, introducing our technology in the best possible way
to more and more potential subscribers who receive those videos, who click on the screen and say, hey, okay, this is sick, this is cool.
I want this. Where did they get this sales tool?</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">If
you think that that tipping point is not coming, then you&rsquo;re not paying attention to the rapid changes in the world around you.
Livestream shopping in China has exploded. In fact, exploded is probably an understatement, with more than 500 million people in China
purchasing products last year through livestream shopping. It&rsquo;s a tsunami, and it&rsquo;s washing over the planet. We&rsquo;re
right there leading this new paradigm in the western world. Because, one, we saw this coming years ago. We were way in front of it and
began developing the technology before almost everyone, and two, our technology is better.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">For
those of you who don&rsquo;t know what these products are, let me provide a quick overview. verbMAIL was developed pursuant to a partnership
we have Microsoft, verbMAIL is an Outlook add on that you can download from the Microsoft online store right now. It places a cool verbMAIL
icon right in your Microsoft Outlook toolbar. Click it and you can create an interactive video with buy it now buttons among many other
clickable icons. Then it automatically places that interactive video right in an email for you that you could send out right through
Outlook.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

sales tool. The current release of verbMail is free to help accelerate adoption and awareness. It gives users a taste of how fun and
effective interactive video emails can be. But it gets better. With the upcoming follow on releases, we&rsquo;ll introduce paid subscription-based
pricing for powerful business features specifically aimed at sales professionals.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Let&rsquo;s
talk about one of these features. When you send your verbMAIL interactive video through Outlook, the moment your customer prospect watches
that video, you&rsquo;ll get a pop-up message on your computer or mobile device notifying you. Some of you are saying right now, wait,
wait, don&rsquo;t you already have that feature in verbCRM? Yes, the answer is yes. But here&rsquo;s where we go next level; that pop-up
message in Outlook not only tells you that your video is being watched by your prospect, but in this version, what&rsquo;s coming, it&rsquo;s
also going to give you the option to click on that pop0up message and decide if you want your prospect to know, while your prospect,
while he or she is watching that video, that you&rsquo;re online and available right then to talk if they&rsquo;d like to.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Now
check this out. If you select that option, a message then pops up on the screen of your prospect while they&rsquo;re watching your video
letting them know you&rsquo;re available in that moment, and if they want to chat with you, they can click on that message. Then it&rsquo;s
going to launch a two-way interactive verbLIVE video session, a Zoom-like session except with Verb&rsquo;s proprietary interactive ecommerce
capability, right there and then while their interest level is piqued. For those who want to connect right then but don&rsquo;t want
to be on camera, they can choose to launch a live real-time chat. We expect this feature to be available for verbMAIL users this year.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Now,
let&rsquo;s talk about livestreaming. verbLIVE is the best livestream shopping platform on the planet. verbLIVE gives everyone the ability
to sell anything from anywhere by broadcasting their own QVC style show right from their mobile device or their computer and while they&rsquo;re
broadcasting live, they can add clickable, shoppable icons right in the video that show up on the screens of all viewers all over the
world, for instant, friction-free buying capability, and we just made it even better with our new attribution feature.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Here&rsquo;s
how it works. Anyone, anyone with a contact list can go into verbLIVE, checkout the upcoming live stream shopping events, and by the
way, this is super, super hot right now in the direct sales space. You can go into the app and select an event, and the app will generate
a special invite for you that you could then share with your entire contact list. You can even post it on social media. When anyone you
shared it with attends that livestream event and purchases something or becomes a member, you get the commission, you get the credit.
That&rsquo;s right, you did nothing more than invite your contacts to someone else&rsquo;s verbLIVE event, and you&rsquo;ve generated
income for yourself.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">With
attribution, we just increased the total addressable market for verbLIVE exponentially, as anyone with a contact list can generate an
income without having to be in front of the camera hosting their own event. Come on, this is game changing. The attribution feature is
Verb&rsquo;s proprietary technology. We designed it and we developed it, and now it&rsquo;s in verbLIVE and being offered as an upgrade
for an additional monthly fee as we speak. We think attribution might be one of the biggest value creation opportunities for our shareholders
going into the second half of this year and into 2022 and beyond.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">All
right, let&rsquo;s talk about PULSE. PULSE is our newest sales enablement feature. It&rsquo;s like a sales coach in your pocket, tracking
your interactions with your prospects, and I mean all of them, it could be hundreds or thousands of them, and telling you what to do
next to close that sale. It&rsquo;s another ground-breaking hyper growth product and we&rsquo;ve delivered all these products in just
the past three months. We began launching paying clients on verbLIVE with attribution. I&rsquo;m talking about large, multinational clients
at the end of June or beginning of July.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Look
for that revenue to begin being recognized on our P&amp;L in third or fourth quarter of this year, and look, I know you want it now,
you want to see it now in our Q2 report. I get it, believe me, I get it. I wanted it in Q2 of last year. Trust me, I&rsquo;m one of the
largest shareholders in this thing, and with my own money in it, and no one is pushing harder and faster to grow this thing. But now,
now the table is set, the technology is real. It&rsquo;s now being used by the sales teams of giant enterprises around the world with
more and more coming on every week. Just in the past few weeks, I&rsquo;m seeing reports of tens of thousands of verbLIVE events being
held all over the world. Based on the results they&rsquo;re getting, the only question now is, how big does this get? How fast and how
big can we grow this? For those of you who know us, you know we dream big. We think big, we like big, okay. Yes, and bigger is definitely
better. It&rsquo;s truly an exciting time to be part of Verb.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Here&rsquo;s

a doubt, it&rsquo;s the biggest and best tool we have ever released to the field.&rdquo; Okay, another boasted of success they were having
with it and shared some of the detailed metrics they would see with it. They said this, &ldquo;60%,&rdquo; okay, six zero, &ldquo;60%
of the people attending their verbLIVE events were purchasing product during the Verb Livestream.&rdquo; Talk about validation. These
comments are coming from the CEOs and Senior Executives of billion-dollar global e-commerce companies, guys.</FONT></P>

SaaS business over the past two years. Think about that. All those revenue catalysts we talked about that have just come online and more
to come this year and into next are not, I repeat, not in that 30% growth rate.</FONT></P>

up 10% over last quarter, up 26% over the same period last year. SaaS recurring revenue as a percentage of total digital revenue was
88% compared with 76% for the same period last year and up over the 81% we reported in Q1 2021.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

and fulfillment side of the business of approximately $400,000 since last year, as that component of our business is, as most of you
probably know, is driven by our clients&rsquo; in-person conferences and sales events, which were essentially nonexistent due to the
continuing effects of COVID. Obviously that has had little to no effect on our current SaaS recurring revenue subscription business,

it actually represents an increase in our subscription-based SaaS recurring revenue of 26% over last year and a reduction in non-SaaS
digital revenue.</FONT></P>

plus our non-SaaS digital revenue and the non-digital revenue stream that, as Rory stated, was slightly off due to the clients not hosting
in-person conferences and conventions.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: Black">Hi,
